After driving from San Diego up to Paso Robles we pulled off the road and discovered this lovely little town of Arroyo Grande. Hungry and ready for a glass of wine, we stumbled upon the Rooster Creek Tavern. The outdoor seating was socially distanced and clean and we settled in. We got the margarhita pizza and a local glass of wine. The service was impeccable, the pizza was delicious with those perfectly sweet Italian tomatoes and fresh basil on top of a delicious crust. A very pleasant surprise and great dinner break after driving all day!<//review>

TF has great flavors and the price fits my wallet.  The one thing that keeps me coming back because TF isn't the closet yogurt shop to me is that they have 4 different sizes of cups and not just 2 like all of the other ones.  Most places have big and giant cups and I always feel like I need to fill it up only to find I can't eat it all and have to throw it away as I don't have any where to freeze it. <Rate>2</Rate>< Text>
If I were only reviewing their equipment quality and ease of use, I would give them five stars.  However, their customer service is another matter.  If the IRS and the DMV got together and had a child and it grew up to provide customer service, that would be Samsara's customer service model.  I've had so many different reps in the few years I've been with them it's laughable, apparently the reason is they're promoting people upward, but it might be in their best interest to not consider their customer rep jobs the lowest ones on the totem pole and try leaving some good ones there.  Furthermore, they nearly refuse to speak with you on the phone.  They prefer everything be done via email, so what used to be done in one phone call now takes a veritable snowstorm of emails.  Finally, if you need to order more equipment, your customer rep no longer handles that for you--which does leave one to wonder what the customer reps are actually there for.  No, it's totally self-service, and you have to find the link within the software to access their store, and then it's a complicated series of clicks to end up with 1)the wrong equipment, or 2)not enough equipment.  Which, of course, leads to another extremely irritating interaction via email with whoever your rep of the day is.  I'm staying with them 100% because the reporting and analytics are top-notch.  I dread any time I find myself having to interact with them.< /Text>

I have been twice to stories in stone and both visits were great. Super friendly, best selection, and well priced. On my first visit I was fortunate enough to talk with one if the owners, Russ. I also overheard him being very patient and informative to a couple who had no interest in minerals but we're in the shop to see if something they had inherited was valuable.

My favorite thing about stories in stones is the learning center that is open for the public to explore. They also host field trips, workshops, and parties (if I remember correctly).

The learning center alone is worth the visit, but it will be difficult to resist the urge to bring something home.</Review>< pictures>

<Review>This is the best rock and fosil store we have ever been to.  We can walk around the store for hours and look at everything more than once.  Everyone that works here is so nice and helpful. On our second trip to the Angel's Camp are my family looked forward to visiting this store more than anything else.  The prices are excellent and the inventory is always being updated. The owner is a wonderful man who truly has a gift for teaching.  He took us into the educational area and have my family a short version of the classes he gives to the school tours that come through. It is very fascinating to learn how much you and your daily life revolve around rocks and elements. The only disappointment we had was on our second visit the owner was not in the shop,  however the couple that was in charge of the store that day were fantastic. They have a wholesale section that is open to the public, you just have to add 50% to the wholesale price. Even with the 50% added on anything you could want is still a bargain. This place is not to be missed if in the Angel's Camp area.  I wish i could give them more than 5 stars we love this place so much.

Be sure to ask about the geode that still has the water in it. Very interesting this geode was never cracked by the earth so the water is still inside.  This rock is incredible. Solid rock sphere with liquid inside this is a must see at the shop.

We have not been here in about two years and we are definitely due for another trip there. I was way overdue for a review of this wonderful place.<//Review><pictures>None</pictures><Resp>None< /Resp>< gmapID>

<review>I went in on a Tuesday afternoon to drop off my Samsung S7 edge that had a blinking green and black sleep mode (standby) screen. Occasionally, when the phone heats up it will flash all white.It wasn't too busy but I had things to do so I left it there for a couple hours. Came back after 3 hours & I was told my phone had corrosion in the charging port & throughout the inside of my phone. I was a little furious because I just got a brand new phone (upgraded from S5) in July. This phone is just 8 weeks old & NO, I DID NOT SUBJECT my phone to any liquids or water. The technician who "opened" my phone was named Sayuri. I can tell I got under her skin because I wanted her to show me the "corrosion" as I assured her that was not the problem. But hey, what do I know, I'm not the " Sprint Certified Technician". She told me it would take 45 minutes to re-open the phone to show me the damage (red  flag #1) also, because it has "Visible water damage" around the phone (again, I asked them to show me where and they were looking at the edge of the screen protector shield! Red flag #2) & they noticed the back of the phone to have had some kind of substance on there. Yeah, It's August people( summer!) Peoples hands sweat & without a case it will show prints of some sort but certainly not a LIQUID substance.Then, she added, IF THERE IS VISIBLE SIGNS OF WATER, LIQUID (or god forbid your phone is dented or scratched) They "ARE NOT REQUIRED TO OPEN THE PHONE AND DIAGNOSE THE PHONE", (per rules of their franchise-RED FLAG #3- which in my case was what pushed me over the edge for further investigation). She continued to say that since the phone is corroded, I would have to pay $200 for a replacement from my insurance. What!? IT'S A NEW PHONE PLUS, Your girl (me) has done her research... go on youtube, or google... you will see other people had this same issue after a few weeks of use. I told her it is a internal problem. She did however say, I can go to Best Buy and have a Samsung representative open the phone for me and show me the damage and have them try to fix it. (THIS IS NOT THE FIRST TIME THESE PEOPLE HAS SENT ME ELSEWHERE FOR A PROBLEM)  So, like an idiot, I go to Best Buy. Any person will know that because the phone was not purchased at BB, they can't fix it. That's exactly what the guy told me. He was a VERY NICE guy however, and did say THIS IS NOT WATER DAMAGE, It is a internal motherboard malfunction. I had to mail the phone to Samsung HQ in TX & it will take 15 days to get a replacement FOR FREE since it's under a manufacture warranty. I need a phone asap so I went all the way to Encinitas Corporate store. Guess what? In about an hour, the tech said it was a motherboard problem and as soon as he opened the phone, the phone completely fried. They were able to order me a replacement FOR FREE! So, Why did this store make me want to pay $200? Why couldn't they help me out like Encinitas did? Why did Sayuri lie to me and said she opened it when she didn't? What was the corrosion she saw? Either these people need their eyes checked, or get a technician that actually looks at phones. I counted on this Sprint store (on Douglas) to be able to help me because they are right around the corner from my home. Instead they send people away to other places. Before this issue, I went in to this store in June because I needed to cancel my account and add me to my husbands account so we can have just 1 bill, they sent me to the corporate store on Vista way because this Douglas store is not able to do a transfer of ownership. The store on Vista way said they are unable to help and that procedure is done online!  Anyways, I went back to Sprint-Douglas & asked for the name and number for the regional manager. The associate went to the back and I guess spoke to another Sprint team member and he came back out and said they are not allowed to give the name and number for the Sprint Regional Manager. WOW!! When it comes to getting a new phone however you always see stores advertising great deals but you always get killed with the fine print. So I always rely on the sales associate word and hope for the best. Ray was everything you could ask for. Ray was extremely knowledgeable on all deals sprint has to offer. There is some fees that make me cringe, activation fee of roughly 30$ specifically. I mean I pay 30$ for them to push a button pretty much (or least that‚Äôs how I see it). But Ray was there to save the day. < text>
I rarely give a full five stars. I often want to give four and a half or three and three quarters stars but this place deserves five. They are exactly what they say they are, a Panaderia.

Yes, they have other Foods, they have delicious hot foods made right there for you as well, ice cream, other market sundries you might need for your food especially if you cook latin-style periodically.

But today I went there for lots of pan, Mexican sweet breads. The lady was really sweet, we spoke in Spanish, the other girls that have helped me there also really awesome.

I've never actually sat down to eat there. I'm usually in a hurry, but you can't beat great Mexican sweetbreads and the price is amazing! Go there. You won't be disappointed. If you want fancy-schmancy go somewhere else. If you want the real deal go here.<//text>

< Text>
This is the best bakery in Merced, Mexican or otherwise. It's not easy to find, they could probably do with a new sign but they are always busy so I guess they don't need it. The baked goods are awesome. I also like the hot food that I have tried so far. The tamales have a perfect meat:masa ratio and everything always tastes fresh which is always a good thing. There's also a little ice cream shop on one side of the store. From outside you wouldn't even know it was a bakery if not for the smell of fresh baked goodness you can smell from a distance. I am sure that those bigger mercado type stores have their benefits but I know where to go to get quality and taste. The prices are even better too!<//Text>

My former dentist,  who retired after 50 years, Dr. Au referred me to D. D. S. Lily Djie at Bonita Point Dental Arts. Dr. Au a stated, I would be in good hands. Immediately after entering the dental office, I was immediately greeted in a friendly welcoming tone by Hygenist Rose. Shortly thereafter I was taken to the dental room for X-Rays. The Dental Assistant Cindy also greeted me in the same manner as Rose, who explained the purpose of the X-Rays. The process was quickly done, each set of the photos taken of my teeth, was displayed on a screen to ensure the photo was taken correctly. Next, I  was seen by the Hygenist Rose, who also explained the process, as she cleaned my teeth she frequently checked on how I was feeling.
Then I was seen by D. D. S. Djie, who also displayed the friendly manner as her employees. She explained in a simple terms the condition of my teeth,  and she did not show signs of being in a hurry and took her time with me.

In closing I want to mention the equipment used are modern and the staff mannerisms are outstanding. If you are hesitant in seeing a dentist, your fears will be toned down after your visit to D.D.S. Lily Djie.<//review>
